### Text Exchange - 2026-01-19 09:22:10 UTC [10:22:10 CEST]

**User Message:** thath's the problem... the key is already in use (as I added it recently)

**Assistant Response:** I see the problem. GitHub doesn't allow the same SSH key on multiple accounts. Your key `gh-lean-mac-personal` is currently registered to your **Frank-Woernle_bmw** account on github.com.

**Solution:**

1. Log into github.com as **Frank-Woernle_bmw**
2. Go to Settings ‚Üí SSH and GPG keys
3. Find and **delete** the key named "gh-lean-mac-personal" (fingerprint `SHA256:<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>gnI`)
4. Log back into **fwornle**
5. Add the key there

Once removed from Frank-Woernle_b...

**Type:** Text-only exchange (no tool calls)

**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/install.sh",
  "old_string": "    download_cgr_cache\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Start Memgraph: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}",
  "new_string": "    download_cgr_cache\n\n    # Reindex CGR cache if stale (requires Docker for Memgraph)\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed() {\n        local staleness_script=\"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR/scripts/check-cache-staleness.sh\"\n        local reindex_script=\"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR/scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n\n        # Check if staleness script exists\n        if [[ ! -x \"$staleness_script\" ]]; then\n            info \"CGR staleness check script not found, skipping reindex\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check cache staleness\n        info \"Checking CGR cache freshness...\"\n        local staleness_json\n        staleness_json=$(\"$staleness_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" 2>/dev/null) || true\n\n        local is_stale=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.is_stale // true' 2>/dev/null)\n        local commits_behind=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.commits_behind // \"unknown\"' 2>/dev/null)\n\n        if [[ \"$is_stale\" != \"true\" ]]; then\n            success \"CGR cache is fresh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"CGR cache is stale ($commits_behind commits behind)\"\n\n        # Check if Docker is available\n        if ! command -v docker &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker not available - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Run manually: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check if Docker daemon is running\n        if ! docker info &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker daemon not running - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Start Docker and run: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"Starting Memgraph for CGR reindex...\"\n        cd \"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR\"\n\n        # Start Memgraph container\n        if ! docker-compose up -d 2>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Failed to start Memgraph - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Wait for Memgraph to be ready (max 30 seconds)\n        info \"Waiting for Memgraph to be ready...\"\n        local max_wait=30\n        local waited=0\n        while ! docker-compose exec -T memgraph mgconsole -c \"RETURN 1\" &>/dev/null; do\n            sleep 1\n            ((waited++))\n            if [[ $waited -ge $max_wait ]]; then\n                warning \"Memgraph not ready after ${max_wait}s - CGR reindex skipped\"\n                cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n                return 0\n            fi\n        done\n\n        success \"Memgraph ready\"\n\n        # Run reindex\n        info \"Reindexing CGR cache (this may take a few minutes)...\"\n        if [[ -x \"$reindex_script\" ]]; then\n            if \"$reindex_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" \"coding\" 2>&1 | tail -5; then\n                success \"CGR cache reindexed successfully\"\n            else\n                warning \"CGR reindex had issues - check logs in integrations/code-graph-rag/shared-data/reindex.log\"\n            fi\n        else\n            warning \"Reindex script not executable\"\n        fi\n\n        cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n    }\n\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}"

-x \"$staleness_script\" ]]; then\n            info \"CGR staleness check script not found, skipping reindex\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check cache staleness\n        info \"Checking CGR cache freshness...\"\n        local staleness_json\n        staleness_json=$(\"$staleness_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" 2>/dev/null) || true\n\n        local is_stale=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.is_stale // true' 2>/dev/null)\n        local commits_behind=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.commits_behind // \"unknown\"' 2>/dev/null)\n\n        if [[ \"$is_stale\" != \"true\" ]]; then\n            success \"CGR cache is fresh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"CGR cache is stale ($commits_behind commits behind)\"\n\n        # Check if Docker is available\n        if ! command -v docker &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker not available - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Run manually: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check if Docker daemon is running\n        if ! docker info &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker daemon not running - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Start Docker and run: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"Starting Memgraph for CGR reindex...\"\n        cd \"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR\"\n\n        # Start Memgraph container\n        if ! docker-compose up -d 2>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Failed to start Memgraph - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Wait for Memgraph to be ready (max 30 seconds)\n        info \"Waiting for Memgraph to be ready...\"\n        local max_wait=30\n        local waited=0\n        while ! docker-compose exec -T memgraph mgconsole -c \"RETURN 1\" &>/dev/null; do\n            sleep 1\n            ((waited++))\n            if [[ $waited -ge $max_wait ]]; then\n                warning \"Memgraph not ready after ${max_wait}s - CGR reindex skipped\"\n                cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n                return 0\n            fi\n        done\n\n        success \"Memgraph ready\"\n\n        # Run reindex\n        info \"Reindexing CGR cache (this may take a few minutes)...\"\n        if [[ -x \"$reindex_script\" ]]; then\n            if \"$reindex_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" \"coding\" 2>&1 | tail -5; then\n                success \"CGR cache reindexed successfully\"\n            else\n                warning \"CGR reindex had issues - check logs in integrations/code-graph-rag/shared-data/reindex.log\"\n            fi\n        else\n            warning \"Reindex script not executable\"\n        fi\n\n        cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n    }\n\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}"
}

docker-compose exec -T memgraph mgconsole -c \"RETURN 1\" &>/dev/null; do\n            sleep 1\n            ((waited++))\n            if [[ $waited -ge $max_wait ]]; then\n                warning \"Memgraph not ready after ${max_wait}s - CGR reindex skipped\"\n                cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n                return 0\n            fi\n        done\n\n        success \"Memgraph ready\"\n\n        # Run reindex\n        info \"Reindexing CGR cache (this may take a few minutes)...\"\n        if [[ -x \"$reindex_script\" ]]; then\n            if \"$reindex_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" \"coding\" 2>&1 | tail -5; then\n                success \"CGR cache reindexed successfully\"\n            else\n                warning \"CGR reindex had issues - check logs in integrations/code-graph-rag/shared-data/reindex.log\"\n            fi\n        else\n            warning \"Reindex script not executable\"\n        fi\n\n        cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n    }\n\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}"
}
```

**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/install.sh",
  "old_string": "    download_cgr_cache\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Start Memgraph: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}",
  "new_string": "    download_cgr_cache\n\n    # Reindex CGR cache if stale (requires Docker for Memgraph)\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed() {\n        local staleness_script=\"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR/scripts/check-cache-staleness.sh\"\n        local reindex_script=\"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR/scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n\n        # Check if staleness script exists\n        if [[ ! -x \"$staleness_script\" ]]; then\n            info \"CGR staleness check script not found, skipping reindex\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check cache staleness\n        info \"Checking CGR cache freshness...\"\n        local staleness_json\n        staleness_json=$(\"$staleness_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" 2>/dev/null) || true\n\n        local is_stale=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.is_stale // true' 2>/dev/null)\n        local commits_behind=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.commits_behind // \"unknown\"' 2>/dev/null)\n\n        if [[ \"$is_stale\" != \"true\" ]]; then\n            success \"CGR cache is fresh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"CGR cache is stale ($commits_behind commits behind)\"\n\n        # Check if Docker is available\n        if ! command -v docker &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker not available - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Run manually: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check if Docker daemon is running\n        if ! docker info &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker daemon not running - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Start Docker and run: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"Starting Memgraph for CGR reindex...\"\n        cd \"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR\"\n\n        # Start Memgraph container\n        if ! docker-compose up -d 2>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Failed to start Memgraph - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Wait for Memgraph to be ready (max 30 seconds)\n        info \"Waiting for Memgraph to be ready...\"\n        local max_wait=30\n        local waited=0\n        while ! docker-compose exec -T memgraph mgconsole -c \"RETURN 1\" &>/dev/null; do\n            sleep 1\n            ((waited++))\n            if [[ $waited -ge $max_wait ]]; then\n                warning \"Memgraph not ready after ${max_wait}s - CGR reindex skipped\"\n                cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n                return 0\n            fi\n        done\n\n        success \"Memgraph ready\"\n\n        # Run reindex\n        info \"Reindexing CGR cache (this may take a few minutes)...\"\n        if [[ -x \"$reindex_script\" ]]; then\n            if \"$reindex_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" \"coding\" 2>&1 | tail -5; then\n                success \"CGR cache reindexed successfully\"\n            else\n                warning \"CGR reindex had issues - check logs in integrations/code-graph-rag/shared-data/reindex.log\"\n            fi\n        else\n            warning \"Reindex script not executable\"\n        fi\n\n        cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n    }\n\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}"
}

### Edit - 2026-01-19 09:44:43 UTC [10:44:43 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/install.sh",
  "old_string": "    download_cgr_cache\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Start Memgraph: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}",
  "new_string": "    download_cgr_cache\n\n    # Reindex CGR cache if stale (requires Docker for Memgraph)\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed() {\n        local staleness_script=\"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR/scripts/check-cache-staleness.sh\"\n        local reindex_script=\"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR/scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n\n        # Check if staleness script exists\n        if [[ ! -x \"$staleness_script\" ]]; then\n            info \"CGR staleness check script not found, skipping reindex\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check cache staleness\n        info \"Checking CGR cache freshness...\"\n        local staleness_json\n        staleness_json=$(\"$staleness_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" 2>/dev/null) || true\n\n        local is_stale=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.is_stale // true' 2>/dev/null)\n        local commits_behind=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.commits_behind // \"unknown\"' 2>/dev/null)\n\n        if [[ \"$is_stale\" != \"true\" ]]; then\n            success \"CGR cache is fresh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"CGR cache is stale ($commits_behind commits behind)\"\n\n        # Check if Docker is available\n        if ! command -v docker &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker not available - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Run manually: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check if Docker daemon is running\n        if ! docker info &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker daemon not running - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Start Docker and run: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"Starting Memgraph for CGR reindex...\"\n        cd \"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR\"\n\n        # Start Memgraph container\n        if ! docker-compose up -d 2>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Failed to start Memgraph - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Wait for Memgraph to be ready (max 30 seconds)\n        info \"Waiting for Memgraph to be ready...\"\n        local max_wait=30\n        local waited=0\n        while ! docker-compose exec -T memgraph mgconsole -c \"RETURN 1\" &>/dev/null; do\n            sleep 1\n            ((waited++))\n            if [[ $waited -ge $max_wait ]]; then\n                warning \"Memgraph not ready after ${max_wait}s - CGR reindex skipped\"\n                cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n                return 0\n            fi\n        done\n\n        success \"Memgraph ready\"\n\n        # Run reindex\n        info \"Reindexing CGR cache (this may take a few minutes)...\"\n        if [[ -x \"$reindex_script\" ]]; then\n            if \"$reindex_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" \"coding\" 2>&1 | tail -5; then\n                success \"CGR cache reindexed successfully\"\n            else\n                warning \"CGR reindex had issues - check logs in integrations/code-graph-rag/shared-data/reindex.log\"\n            fi\n        else\n            warning \"Reindex script not executable\"\n        fi\n\n        cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n    }\n\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}"

-x \"$staleness_script\" ]]; then\n            info \"CGR staleness check script not found, skipping reindex\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check cache staleness\n        info \"Checking CGR cache freshness...\"\n        local staleness_json\n        staleness_json=$(\"$staleness_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" 2>/dev/null) || true\n\n        local is_stale=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.is_stale // true' 2>/dev/null)\n        local commits_behind=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.commits_behind // \"unknown\"' 2>/dev/null)\n\n        if [[ \"$is_stale\" != \"true\" ]]; then\n            success \"CGR cache is fresh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"CGR cache is stale ($commits_behind commits behind)\"\n\n        # Check if Docker is available\n        if ! command -v docker &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker not available - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Run manually: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check if Docker daemon is running\n        if ! docker info &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker daemon not running - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Start Docker and run: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"Starting Memgraph for CGR reindex...\"\n        cd \"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR\"\n\n        # Start Memgraph container\n        if ! docker-compose up -d 2>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Failed to start Memgraph - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Wait for Memgraph to be ready (max 30 seconds)\n        info \"Waiting for Memgraph to be ready...\"\n        local max_wait=30\n        local waited=0\n        while ! docker-compose exec -T memgraph mgconsole -c \"RETURN 1\" &>/dev/null; do\n            sleep 1\n            ((waited++))\n            if [[ $waited -ge $max_wait ]]; then\n                warning \"Memgraph not ready after ${max_wait}s - CGR reindex skipped\"\n                cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n                return 0\n            fi\n        done\n\n        success \"Memgraph ready\"\n\n        # Run reindex\n        info \"Reindexing CGR cache (this may take a few minutes)...\"\n        if [[ -x \"$reindex_script\" ]]; then\n            if \"$reindex_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" \"coding\" 2>&1 | tail -5; then\n                success \"CGR cache reindexed successfully\"\n            else\n                warning \"CGR reindex had issues - check logs in integrations/code-graph-rag/shared-data/reindex.log\"\n            fi\n        else\n            warning \"Reindex script not executable\"\n        fi\n\n        cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n    }\n\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}"

-x \"$staleness_script\" ]]; then\n            info \"CGR staleness check script not found, skipping reindex\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check cache staleness\n        info \"Checking CGR cache freshness...\"\n        local staleness_json\n        staleness_json=$(\"$staleness_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" 2>/dev/null) || true\n\n        local is_stale=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.is_stale // true' 2>/dev/null)\n        local commits_behind=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.commits_behind // \"unknown\"' 2>/dev/null)\n\n        if [[ \"$is_stale\" != \"true\" ]]; then\n            success \"CGR cache is fresh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"CGR cache is stale ($commits_behind commits behind)\"\n\n        # Check if Docker is available\n        if !   "new_string": "    download_cgr_cache\n\n    # Reindex CGR cache if stale (requires Docker for Memgraph)\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed() {\n        local staleness_script=\"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR/scripts/check-cache-staleness.sh\"\n        local reindex_script=\"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR/scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n\n        # Check if staleness script exists\n        if [[ ! -x \"$staleness_script\" ]]; then\n            info \"CGR staleness check script not found, skipping reindex\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check cache staleness\n        info \"Checking CGR cache freshness...\"\n        local staleness_json\n        staleness_json=$(\"$staleness_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" 2>/dev/null) || true\n\n        local is_stale=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.is_stale // true' 2>/dev/null)\n        local commits_behind=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.commits_behind // \"unknown\"' 2>/dev/null)\n\n        if [[ \"$is_stale\" != \"true\" ]]; then\n            success \"CGR cache is fresh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"CGR cache is stale ($commits_behind commits behind)\"\n\n        # Check if Docker is available\n        if ! command -v docker &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker not available - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Run manually: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check if Docker daemon is running\n        if ! docker info &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker daemon not running - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Start Docker and run: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"Starting Memgraph for CGR reindex...\"\n        cd \"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR\"\n\n        # Start Memgraph container\n        if ! docker-compose up -d 2>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Failed to start Memgraph - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Wait for Memgraph to be ready (max 30 seconds)\n        info \"Waiting for Memgraph to be ready...\"\n        local max_wait=30\n        local waited=0\n        while ! docker-compose exec -T memgraph mgconsole -c \"RETURN 1\" &>/dev/null; do\n            sleep 1\n            ((waited++))\n            if [[ $waited -ge $max_wait ]]; then\n                warning \"Memgraph not ready after ${max_wait}s - CGR reindex skipped\"\n                cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n                return 0\n            fi\n        done\n\n        success \"Memgraph ready\"\n\n        # Run reindex\n        info \"Reindexing CGR cache (this may take a few minutes)...\"\n        if [[ -x \"$reindex_script\" ]]; then\n            if \"$reindex_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" \"coding\" 2>&1 | tail -5; then\n                success \"CGR cache reindexed successfully\"\n            else\n                warning \"CGR reindex had issues - check logs in integrations/code-graph-rag/shared-data/reindex.log\"\n            fi\n        else\n            warning \"Reindex script not executable\"\n        fi\n\n        cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n    }\n\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}"

-x \"$staleness_script\" ]]; then\n            info \"CGR staleness check script not found, skipping reindex\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check cache staleness\n        info \"Checking CGR cache freshness...\"\n        local staleness_json\n        staleness_json=$(\"$staleness_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" 2>/dev/null) || true\n\n        local is_stale=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.is_stale // true' 2>/dev/null)\n        local commits_behind=$(echo \"$staleness_json\" | jq -r '.commits_behind // \"unknown\"' 2>/dev/null)\n\n        if [[ \"$is_stale\" != \"true\" ]]; then\n            success \"CGR cache is fresh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"CGR cache is stale ($commits_behind commits behind)\"\n\n        # Check if Docker is available\n        if ! command -v docker &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker not available - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Run manually: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Check if Docker daemon is running\n        if ! docker info &>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Docker daemon not running - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            info \"  Start Docker and run: cd integrations/code-graph-rag && docker-compose up -d && ./scripts/reindex-with-metadata.sh\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        info \"Starting Memgraph for CGR reindex...\"\n        cd \"$CODE_GRAPH_RAG_DIR\"\n\n        # Start Memgraph container\n        if ! docker-compose up -d 2>/dev/null; then\n            warning \"Failed to start Memgraph - CGR reindex skipped\"\n            cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n            return 0\n        fi\n\n        # Wait for Memgraph to be ready (max 30 seconds)\n        info \"Waiting for Memgraph to be ready...\"\n        local max_wait=30\n        local waited=0\n        while ! docker-compose exec -T memgraph mgconsole -c \"RETURN 1\" &>/dev/null; do\n            sleep 1\n            ((waited++))\n            if [[ $waited -ge $max_wait ]]; then\n                warning \"Memgraph not ready after ${max_wait}s - CGR reindex skipped\"\n                cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n                return 0\n            fi\n        done\n\n        success \"Memgraph ready\"\n\n        # Run reindex\n        info \"Reindexing CGR cache (this may take a few minutes)...\"\n        if [[ -x \"$reindex_script\" ]]; then\n            if \"$reindex_script\" \"$CODING_REPO\" \"coding\" 2>&1 | tail -5; then\n                success \"CGR cache reindexed successfully\"\n            else\n                warning \"CGR reindex had issues - check logs in integrations/code-graph-rag/shared-data/reindex.log\"\n            fi\n        else\n            warning \"Reindex script not executable\"\n        fi\n\n        cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n    }\n\n    reindex_cgr_if_needed\n\n    success \"code-graph-rag installed\"\n    info \"  - Memgraph Lab: http://localhost:3100\"\n    info \"  - MCP server: uv run graph-code mcp-server\"\n\n    cd \"$CODING_REPO\"\n}"

### Edit - 2026-01-19 09:50:40 UTC [10:50:40 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/lib/api-quota-checker.js",
  "old_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota (free tier, rate-limited)\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Groq doesn't have a usage endpoint - free tier with rate limits only\n  // Show as \"free\" indicator since there's no credit tracking\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: null, // No credit tracking for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}",
  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
}
```

### Edit - 2026-01-19 09:50:40 UTC [10:50:40 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/lib/api-quota-checker.js",
  "old_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota (free tier, rate-limited)\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Groq doesn't have a usage endpoint - free tier with rate limits only\n  // Show as \"free\" indicator since there's no credit tracking\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: null, // No credit tracking for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}",
  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
}
```

  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
}
```

  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
}
```

**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/lib/api-quota-checker.js",
  "old_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota (free tier, rate-limited)\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Groq doesn't have a usage endpoint - free tier with rate limits only\n  // Show as \"free\" indicator since there's no credit tracking\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: null, // No credit tracking for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}",
  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
}

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/lib/api-quota-checker.js",
  "old_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota (free tier, rate-limited)\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Groq doesn't have a usage endpoint - free tier with rate limits only\n  // Show as \"free\" indicator since there's no credit tracking\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: null, // No credit tracking for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}",
  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
}
```

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/lib/api-quota-checker.js",
  "old_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota (free tier, rate-limited)\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Groq doesn't have a usage endpoint - free tier with rate limits only\n  // Show as \"free\" indicator since there's no credit tracking\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: null, // No credit tracking for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}",
  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
}

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/lib/api-quota-checker.js",
  "old_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota (free tier, rate-limited)\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Groq doesn't have a usage endpoint - free tier with rate limits only\n  // Show as \"free\" indicator since there's no credit tracking\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: null, // No credit tracking for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}",
  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
}
```

{
  "replace_all": false,

  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
}

  "replace_all": false,

  "old_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota (free tier, rate-limited)\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Groq doesn't have a usage endpoint - free tier with rate limits only\n  // Show as \"free\" indicator since there's no credit tracking\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: null, // No credit tracking for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}",
  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
}

  "new_string": "/**\n * Check Groq API quota\n * Free tier: 7.2M tokens/day, 14.4K requests/min\n * Paid tier: Prepaid credits (no public usage API yet)\n *\n * Note: Groq doesn't have a public billing API yet (feature request pending).\n * For paid plans, we use config-based prepaid credits tracking.\n * Set provider_credits.groq.prepaidCredits in live-logging-config.json\n */\nasync function checkGroqQuota(config, timeout) {\n  const apiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;\n  if (!apiKey) return null;\n\n  // Check if user has prepaid credits configured (paid plan)\n  const prepaidCredits = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.prepaidCredits;\n  const hasPrepaidConfig = prepaidCredits !== null && prepaidCredits !== undefined && prepaidCredits > 0;\n\n  if (hasPrepaidConfig) {\n    // Paid plan - show balance from config\n    // Note: Groq doesn't have a usage API, so we can't track actual spend\n    // For now, show the configured prepaid amount as available\n    // TODO: When Groq adds usage API, fetch actual spend and calculate remaining\n    const estimatedUsed = config?.provider_credits?.groq?.estimatedUsed || 0;\n    const remainingCredits = Math.max(0, prepaidCredits - estimatedUsed);\n    const remaining = Math.round((remainingCredits / prepaidCredits) * 100);\n\n    return {\n      provider: 'groq',\n      name: 'Groq',\n      abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n      status: remaining > 10 ? 'healthy' : remaining > 0 ? 'low' : 'critical',\n      quota: {\n        remaining: remaining,\n        remainingCredits: remainingCredits,\n        used: `$${estimatedUsed.toFixed(2)}`,\n        limit: `$${prepaidCredits}`,\n        unit: 'USD'\n      },\n      cost: {\n        total: estimatedUsed,\n        currency: 'USD',\n        note: 'Prepaid balance (Groq has no usage API yet - check console.groq.com for actual spend)'\n      },\n      rateLimit: null, // Paid plans have higher limits\n      lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n      cacheStrategy: 'config-estimate'\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Free tier - show rate limit status with pie symbol\n  return {\n    provider: 'groq',\n    name: 'Groq',\n    abbrev: PROVIDER_ABBREV.groq,\n    status: 'healthy',\n    quota: {\n      remaining: 100, // Assume full availability for free tier\n      used: 'free',\n      limit: '7.2M tokens/day',\n      unit: 'rate-limited'\n    },\n    cost: null, // Free tier\n    rateLimit: {\n      requestsPerMinute: 14400,\n      tokensPerDay: 7200000\n    },\n    lastChecked: new Date().toISOString(),\n    cacheStrategy: 'free-tier'\n  };\n}"
